BEN � Basic problems

 

1.    BEN not receiving any messages

Problem is normally Integration related a= nd has to investigate. Liaise with ICOE and BEN administrator at the region.<= /o:p>

2.    BEN rejecting messages from integration bus. (Normally reported by ICOE)

Login to the region BEN application serve= r and check for transactional dead-letter messages. (Remember to refresh).

�= If there are any, purge all of them and restart the BEN and Scheduler services.=

In the Server Manager go to Features � Me= ssage Queueing � System Queues � Transactional dead-letter me= ssages .

Refresh

If there are any got= o more Actions � All Tasks � Purge

Once this is clear it should be a good id= ea to restart the BEN service and the Scheduler Service.

3.    BEN Reports not executing

This happens when there was some slowdown= on the server, at the time of the report executing at its scheduled time, and = the report query times out. The report data is extracted from the LastRuntime to current time.

�= If this period becomes to long, the data period becomes= too long and time out happens every time. At this stage it is necessary to chan= ge the LastRunTime in the database on the SQL Server<= /span>.

You will need to do an update query as in= the example.

Good idea is to copy the text in the LastRunTime field and obser= ve the Id for the report

Then create a new query as follows (paste= the copied datetime) and modify in this query<= /o:p>

Change the date so the next run will capt= ure 24 hrs of data.

Important : Ver= ify the query is correct before executing !

Verify with end user the next day if the = report executed.

 

4.    SMS�s not being sent

This could be due to a number of factors.=

Check or ask the administrator to check i= f both services are up and running (BEN Service and Scheduler Service)<= /span>

Ask administrator to check if Moxa device and modem in working and online)
